riad gods, correct?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">虽然一开始这对于八百万神中最强者来说，也不过只是一种不切实际的妄想？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_5-33" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage The world.<br>Existence itself.<br>If only I could prune the Tree of Aspects.<br>If only this was an ethereal saw, pruning the aspects or existence<br>Maybe you should regret<br>Breaking my heart. But now, we can make you under stand that<br>You didn’t need to do it.<br>This is the story of a girl who was not content to take the incongruity of existence lying down.<br>Hearts will never be broken again.<br>My thoughts will follow you into your dreams.<br></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">曾经爱过但又失去会比不置爱过要好吗?<br>荒谬至极，吾情愿从未对君动心。<br><br>君之愿，依然是想浪费别人的时间吗?<br>抑或是让曾经爱过君的人后悔不已?<br><br>我之憧憬，我之愿望，<br>游遍幻想乡至尽头，向世界展示我之挚爱。<br><br>我不能自己，我情不自禁，<br>唯有划破我之存在界限，以命相抵。<br><br>我愤怒却无处宣世，<br>于境遇，于世界，于存在自身。<br><br>若我修此相之树如愿以偿，<br>若此相之树修世界如愿以偿。<br><br>君本应悔恨伤我之心，<br>现如今只需丢弃，因为没有意义。<br><br>这是一个女孩的心路历程，<br>她不满足于放下不和谐的存在。<br><br>至此，心灵不会再受到伤害。<br>我之思绪将随君消敬于君之梦中。<br></div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="Stage_6-219" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,219&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem"><a href="./灯笼坂爱美.md" title="灯笼坂爱美">灯笼坂爱美</a> 复活</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-220" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,220&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Did you think it wouldn't occur tous to modify the spell card rules?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">难道你们就没有想过，我们没有考虑过修改符卡规则吗？<br></div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-221" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,221&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...!!!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">……！！！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-222" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,222&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Well, they're mostly the same. Meaning is still power, and all that.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">好吧，其实还是差不多的，因为符卡规则的意义就在于力量，之类的。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-223" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,223&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">We just made it so that intention, in addition to meaning, can confer power and affect the rules of engagement.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">我们将其改成了除了意义本身之外，意图还可以赋予力量影响决斗规则。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-224" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,224&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Creating a better reality is the most powerful intention of all.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">创造一个更美好的世界，是最强大的意图！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" explicit in the rules that since our intentions don't entail causing an incident,</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">但是我们的规则里已经写了，我们并不是想要去引发异变。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-226" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,226&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">这也就是为什么，我们符卡水平一般，但是你们仍然会陷入苦战之中。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-230" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,230&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" to understand.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">比起解决这种小规模冲突没有什么可以让我感到更开心的了。所以，请你们，试着来理解吧。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-231" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage An age without bloodshed.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">符卡规则开启了幻想乡的黄金时代——人与妖怪和谐共存，没有流血的时代。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-232" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,232&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">That break through and all others were aimed at the same goal that Kiseki and I have: making a better world.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">而这一突破和我还有剪世树的意图也不谋而合：让这个世界更加美好。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-233" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,233&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-234" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,234&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-235" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,235&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I admit I have absolutely no idea what I'm supposed to do now.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">我现在也不知道自己要做什么了。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-236" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,236&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Really? ## Ending No. 04

- <font color="Red"> **剧透提示:  *以下内容包含详细故事情节，请自行决定是否继续阅读* ** </font>




<table><tbody><tr class="tt-bgm" id="Ending_No._04-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,1&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-bgm" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">BGM: Waking Up from a Waking Dream</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">BGM: 白日梦醒</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-2" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,2&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">In spite of Aimi and Kiseki's schemes in bending the rules of reality, the confrontation ended in a victory for Gensokyo's incident-resolvers.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">即便爱美和剪世树造成了扭曲真实的异变，幻想乡的城管还是取得了最终的胜利。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-3" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,3&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Kasen could tell Aimi wasn't in the right state of mind to talk things over, so she arranged for a meeting at the Hakurei Shrine the next morning. She and Reimu would discuss the technicalities of reversing the incident with Aimi and Kiseki.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">华扇能感受到爱美现在心态爆炸，完全无法交涉，所以她选择在第二天在博丽神社组织一场会议，她将与灵梦及异变的主谋们讨论如何回溯这场异变。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-4" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,4&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Kasen also invited Nunokae to explain what happened when she met the masterminds, and Marisa and Sanae decided to attend as well.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">她还邀请了布返来讲讲遇到幕后主使后发生了什么，魔理沙和早苗也决定参加。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-5" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,5&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Having had the night to reflect, Aimi explained why she wanted to rewrite reality. Kasen's conclusion was that Aimi's motivations were more complex than "creating a better world" or "making Rikuto love her again". While she may have started with selfish intentions, she also had a genuine desire to change the world for the better.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">花了一晚上来回想发生了什么，爱美向大家解释了为什么她想重塑现实。华扇的结论是爱美的动机远远不止只是“为了创造一个更好的世界”还是“让陆斗重新爱她”这两种想法而已。可能她最开始的动机确实是自私的，但她最后确实想让世界变得更好的。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-6" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,6&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Gradually, Aimi warmed up to the idea of finding other ways to show her love for the world. Reimu and Nunokae agreed to help catch her and Kiseki up on spell card experience, and Reimu offered to let them visit the shrine whenever they liked.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">渐渐的，爱美也萌生了寻找梦逻辑之外能向世界表达爱意的方法的想法，灵梦和布返也同意帮她和剪世树补习符卡功课，灵梦还邀请她们随时来神社做客。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-7" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,7&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">After Aimi finally admitted her actions had been a mistake, Marisa gave her some advice on thinking with a clear head. Sakuya even stopped by to make sure Aimi and Kiseki knew about a method to preserve Kiseki's existence as a tsukumogami after the dream logic disappeared from Gensokyo.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">终于在爱美承认自己的错误行为后，魔理沙给了他一些保持清醒思考的建议，咲夜也到访指导爱美和剪世树关于梦逻辑消失后如何让剪世树继续作为付丧神存在的办法。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-8" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,8&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"So, um...when Kiseki gets a new source of magic...will she still have the ability to change the aspects of existence?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"所以，呃...当剪世树更换了能量来源后，她还拥有改变物体相位的能力吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-9" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,9&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I wouldn't think so. If her power is coming from a new object rather than your emotions, her abilities will come from that object."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我觉得不会了，因为如果她的力量那时来自于这个新物件而不是你的情绪，那她的能力就会由那物件所决定了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-10" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,10&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Oh. Well...that's good then. No more temptation, right?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"哦...嗯...那就挺好的，那改变世界的诱惑也一去不复返了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-11" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,11&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Aimi chuckled nervously as Reimu gave her a reassuring smile.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">爱美紧张的笑了笑，而灵梦尝试用微笑来使她安心。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-12" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,12&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I know you're still a little unsure about this, but we'll work it out."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我明白现在你还有些不确定，但我们会找到解决方法的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-13" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,13&#93;"><td id="天白鹭剪世树" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">天白鹭剪世树</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"The power of moving and being able to cut branches on my own is something I'll still have. I can continue to help you with that."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我仍然还有自己移动和切断树枝的能力，也可以继续帮助你工作的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-14" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,14&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Oh yeah, that's true."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊，那确实没错。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-15" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,15&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yeah, I was wonderin' about that. You said you always had to saw those branches and take 'em to the woodshop, right?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"是，我也在想这个，你说你的工作就是锯掉树枝带到木工店对吧？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-16" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,16&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Was Kiseki still doin' that while you two were causing the dream logic?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你们在发起梦逻辑异变的时候剪世树还能砍树？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-17" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,17&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yes. I was afraid of what everyone at the shop would think about my saw becoming a youkai, so I never told them. I just got a new saw and acted like nothing changed."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"是的，当时我也害怕店里的人会觉得我的锯子变成了妖怪，所以我就买了个新的假装什么都没发生。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-18" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,18&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Kiseki and I could get the job done a lot faster working together, so we split our time between that and crafting our Tree of Aspects."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"剪世树和我一起干活的时候效率很高，所以我们可以有效地分配工作和创造相之树的事宜。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-19" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,19&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"So were you going to tell them about her at some point?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"所以到了某个时候你还是要告诉他们关于剪世树的事情吧？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-20" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,20&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I don't really know. I think I'll have to wait to decide about that until we put reality back to normal."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我真的不确定，我想还得等着我们让现实恢复正常后再说吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-21" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,21&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Understandable."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"嗯，完全可以理解。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-22" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,22&#93;"><td id="雪村布返" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雪村布返</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Hey Aimi, you don't have to spend as much time cutting those branches now that Kiseki's helping you, right? That means you have more time to practice your spell cards and stuff. Maybe you could even split your duties and get another job! Just something that came to me."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊爱美，有了剪世树的帮助你砍树的时间大大缩小了对吧，这意味着你有更多的时间练习符卡和做其他的事情了。甚至你们可以分一下工再打一份工也好啊，这是咱的想法。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-23" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,23&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"That's a good idea! The two of us working together could probably support ourselves. What do you think, Kiseki?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"这点子真不错！我们要是可以精诚合作估计就能养活自己了。你觉得怎么样剪世树？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-24" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,24&#93;"><td id="天白鹭剪世树" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">天白鹭剪世树</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I was designed for cutting trees, so I would love to continue sawing and crafting if that is what we need. You could be free to find something you enjoy more."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我本身就是为了砍树而生的，若需要的话我很乐意继续砍树做木工，爱美你可以去找你想做的更喜欢的工作。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-25" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,25&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"It'll depend on how much we tell them about you, I guess. But I think we could figure something out."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"这大抵取决于我们告诉他们多少关于你的事情，不过办法总比困难多嘛。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-26" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,26&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">With everyone seemingly in high spirits, Kasen took the opportunity to wrap up.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">大家的情绪都很雀跃，华扇趁机收尾了会议。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-27" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,27&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"It seems that we've settled just about everything. Thank you, everyone, for helping out."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"看起来能解决的都解决了，谢谢大家的参与与帮助。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-28" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,28&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">She walked closer to the shrine and sat down next to Aimi.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">她走近神社并坐在了爱美的身边。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-29" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,29&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I think you're handling your part very well, Aimi, but there's one final thought I want to leave you with."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"咱觉得关于你的部分我们处理得很不错，但我还有最后一件事要说。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-30" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,30&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"While you're adjusting back to normal life, please keep it in mind to treat Kiseki with kindness and support. She was once an inanimate tool that you could wield as you desired, but she's now a person, with everything that being a person carries. It sounds like you'll still be helping each other out, and that's great. Just remember to respect her and properly accommodate her desires."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"在你调整回你的正常生活时，请一定要记住友善地支持剪世树，她曾是你可以任意使用的无生命的道具，但现在她是个人了，人的七情六欲在她身上也不会例外。现在看来你们仍然在互相扶持，这很好，只是记得一定要尊重她的人格和选择，并适当满足她的欲望。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-31" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,31&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Of course. Kiseki is my best friend. I'll always do my best for her."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那是肯定的，剪世树是我最好的朋友，我会为她尽心尽力的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-32" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,32&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I think Aimi understands that, really. Remember her big monologue? She was always saying 'WE understand how you want your dreams to come true' or 'WE are creating a new world'. She always included Kiseki. And I have something else to tell you, Aimi."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我相信爱美肯定明白的，还记得她之前的那一段长独白吗？她一直用‘我们明白你想让梦想成真’或是‘我们要创建新世界’，她从来都把剪世树当成团队的一员啊，啊对了爱美，我还有件事要告诉你。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-33" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,33&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"You said you were honored to meet the incident-resolvers of Gensokyo. Well, I'm honored to meet someone who admires what I do. You mentioned me by name when you talked about Gensokyo's protectors! When I first arrived in Gensokyo, I was such an awkward newbie to stuff like youkai and everyone being able to use magic. Could I ever have guessed that I'd meet someone like you?!"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你说见到幻想乡的城管很荣幸对吧，啊，我对于欣赏我的工作的人是同样的感情哦，当你谈到幻想乡的守护者时提到了我的名字哎！我刚到幻想乡的时候，对于妖怪和魔法什么的都是不折不扣的菜鸟啊，当时的我怎能想到会遇见你这种人呢？！"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-34" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,34&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I even started out by causing an incident, just like you. So if I could end up being a defender of Gensokyo, so can you. Maybe, after you're strong enough, you can help resolve a real incident. But that's not the only way to make a positive difference. You can do that with something as small as being a friend to Kiseki and helping her adjust to life in Gensokyo."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"咱一开始也像你一样是异变的黑幕，我后来打算守护幻想乡，这你也同样做得到的啊，当你变得足够强时，你也可以成为真正的解决异变的城管啊！但这也不是你能做的唯一的正面的事情嘛，我觉得当剪世树的朋友并帮她适应幻想乡也是很重要的工作呢！。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-35" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,35&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"And Kiseki, I want you to know that you're so lucky to have a best friend like Aimi. She might've been a little confused about how to express it, but as far as I've seen, her love for others is so genuine and powerful. As long as she thinks things over, I believe she'll never let anyone down."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"还有剪世树啊，我想让你知道有一个像爱美这样的挚友简直太幸运了，可能她对于自己的感情解释起来有些困惑，但就我对她的感受来说，她对别人的爱意是如此的真诚和强大啊！只要她能考虑清楚事情，我相信她的热忱永不会让任何人失望。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-36" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,36&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"And this doesn't have to be the last you see of any of us. I know both of you are going to visit Reimu's shrine sometimes, but you're always welcome at the Moriya Shrine too. And anything you need to be a better incident-resolver of Gensokyo...or anything at all, really...is something I'm willing to help you with."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"这不会是我们最后一次见面的，我知道你们有时会去拜访博丽神社，但守矢神社也一样永远欢迎你们，如果你有对于如何成为城管或是其他任何事情有问题，那我都会很愿意帮忙的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-37" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,37&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I'm seriously so touched to hear that, Sanae. I was worried I'd started out on the wrong foot with all the heroes I admire, but you're so willing to look past my mistakes."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我真心被你的话语打动了，早苗啊，我还担心我和我崇拜的英雄走的是不一样的道路呢，感谢你愿意如此不计前嫌。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-38" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,38&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Hey, I mean, maybe it's that extra kindness you gave us. But it doesn't feel strange now that I have it, so who cares? I'll just roll with it!"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"咱的意思是，可能这份善良也来自于你的梦逻辑吧，拥有善意也不奇怪了，但那谁关心呢，随它去吧！"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-39" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,39&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">The meeting began to adjourn as the girls headed back to their usual places. Sanae was happy that Aimi came to terms with her mistake and left off on a good note with all the incident-resolvers she looked up to, but she couldn't tell herself she didn't have an ulterior motive for wanting to see Aimi more.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">会议收尾后少女们返回了她们的住所，早苗很高兴爱美最后认识到了错误并且最后留下了对城管的向往，但她可没有告诉爱美自己想见她也还有一个秘密的理由。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-40" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,40&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Ever since coming to Gensokyo from the Outside World, Sanae had been surrounded by gods and youkai. She got to see Reimu and Marisa sometimes, but it wouldn't hurt to have another human friend.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">自从来幻想乡后，早苗身边就都是神明和妖怪了，她有时能见到灵梦魔理沙，但再多一个人类朋友肯定好得不得了。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-41" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,41&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">As she thought about this, Sanae remembered the odd emotion-reader in the black dress. She lived just a flight down the mountain from Sanae, but Sanae wasn't actually sure if she was a human or youkai. The humans who lived in far-off places outside the village tended to be the more...eccentric types. More youkai-like humans, in a sense. Could she be one of those?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">她在思考这事的时候想起了那个黑衣的可以阅读情绪的少女，她住在离妖怪山不远的地方，但早苗也不确定她是人类还是妖怪，这类居住在荒无人烟的地方的人类通常都比较...怪，更像妖怪一些，这么想的话她很可能也是其中的一个。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-42" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,42&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Sanae didn't want to aggravate that girl by talking to her again, but her curiosity got the better of her. And maybe that dream-logical desire to think more about other people, too. On the way back home, Sanae stopped in the forest around the mountain's foot to see if she could find the black-clad empath again.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">早苗不想去激怒这女孩，但好奇心战胜了这种心理，可能这也有梦逻辑让大家变得更加关心别人的影响吧。在回家的路上早苗顺道停在了山脚下的森林去寻找那黑衣的共情者。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-43" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,43&#93;"><td id="铃仙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铃仙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Is something over there?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那边有什么吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-44" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,44&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Another one of the interesting people is curious about me too."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊，那些有趣的人之中的一位貌似对我也有了兴趣。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-45" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,45&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Oh, dear. Reisen was already with her, and the empath had already sensed Sanae's presence. But did this mean she was fine with Reisen being there? Sanae stepped out from behind the large bush she was using for cover.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">天哪，铃仙已经和她在一块了，而且那共情者早就感受到了早苗的存在，但这是不是意味着她已经可以默许了铃仙在她身边了？早苗从她用作掩护的大灌木丛里钻了出来。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-46" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,46&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Is this a bad time?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"抱歉，我来的是不是不是时候？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-47" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,47&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Reisen looked at the empath nervously, apparently wanting her to be the one who answered.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铃仙紧张地望着那共情者，显然希望她来回答这个问题。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-48" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,48&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"No. It isn't a bad time. She just feels a bit lonely and is wondering if it's possible for her to have a positive interaction with me."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"不，来得正是时候，她只是觉得孤单寂寞了想看看我可不可以和她做朋友。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-49" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,49&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Sanae flinched, then put on a defeated smile.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">早苗退后几步，然后嘴角挂上了被打败的笑容。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-50" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,50&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"...Well! I guess I don't need to explain why I'm here, then."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"...那我想我也不用解释为什么我来了吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-51" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,51&#93;"><td id="铃仙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铃仙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Tetsuko, for how much you claim not to be interested in other people, there sure are a lot of people who find you interesting."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"不管你怎么宣称对其他人不感兴趣，但其实有很多人对你很感兴趣啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-52" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,52&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"You're name's Tetsuko? Nice to meet you. I'm Sanae. Although you probably picked that up during our...ahem...previous encounter."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你叫铁子？很高兴认识你，我叫早苗，这名字在我们...呃...上一次见面的时候你大概就知道了吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-53" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,53&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"The amanojaku isn't with you this time."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那天邪鬼这次没和你一起来啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-54" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,54&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yeah, her. Just forget about her. It was the dream logic messing with my mind. She was the mastermind of the incident before this one, can you believe that? I was so dead-set on resolving the incident that I felt like I had to make her prove beyond a doubt she wasn't up to no good again."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"对，她。啊忘了她吧。和她同行的我一定是被梦逻辑搞乱了脑袋，知道吗，她可是上一个异变的黑幕哎？！我当时太在乎这个异变了以至于没注意这一点，现在我觉得我必须让她再证明自己确实不会再干坏事了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-55" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,55&#93;"><td id="铃仙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铃仙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"You know, Sanae, just about everyone's personalities were changed by the dream logic, but Seija was pretty much still herself, wasn't she? Do you think that's because her personality was so...um...exotic, to begin with?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"早苗啊，几乎每个人的性格都因为梦逻辑而改变了，但正邪几乎没有变啊不是吗？你觉得是因为她的性格本来就很...奇特吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-56" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,56&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"It could be. Aimi and Kiseki had to manipulate tons of little bits and pieces of our minds to get us to act the way they wanted. Maybe they couldn't change Seija because none of those pieces even applied to her."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"可能吧，爱美和剪世树为了让我们做她们想做的事情需要控制我们意识中的成千上万的小碎片。她们无法改变正邪的原因可能是这些小碎片根本对不上号。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-57" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,57&#93;"><td id="铃仙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铃仙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"That's what I thought. Almost everyone was affected, but I think I'd say the youkai were affected a little less than the humans. Aimi probably had to base the changes she made on her knowledge of her own mind. So the more un-human-like someone's mindset is, the less they'd be changed. That's my hypothesis, anyway. Take it or don't."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我就是这么想的，虽然大家都几乎被影响了，但我觉得妖怪被影响的程度比人类低一些，爱美估计得基于她自己的意识碎片来进行对每个人的改变。所以一个人的思想越不像人类，他们的改变就会越小，这是我的假说啦，你们也可以有别的想法。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-58" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,58&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I think it's my turn to be curious about something. What DID the mastermind want, in the end? Don't most incidents inconvenience people? Did Aimi really just want people to think more about others?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我觉得该轮到我的好奇心来询问了，最后黑幕到底想要什么啊？难道绝大部分异变不是为人们造成不便吗？爱美真的就只是希望人们互相关心得更多吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-59" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,59&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Well, it was a little more complicated than that."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"关于这个啊，其实稍微复杂一些的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-60" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,60&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"There was all this stuff about wanting to RESOLVE incidents, and how Aimi was too busy and not strong enough to do that, and this boy she met who wanted to learn spell cards, and she ended up falling in love with him, but he broke her heart..."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"关于她想当城管解决异变的却太忙也无力的事情，爱美认识的那个想学习符卡的男孩子，最终与他坠入爱河但是他伤了她的心之类的事情..."</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-61" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,61&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"...and she was sad that her dreams couldn't come true, and she wanted the world to be different so people's dreams could come true, and then her pruning saw became a tsukumogami because of the Miracle Mallet incident, which I forgot to mention, and, well..."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"...她很伤心她的梦想无法成真，所以她想要一个大家的梦想都能成真的世界，然后她的修枝锯因为万宝槌变成了付丧神，我忘了提这件事了，还有..."</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-62" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,62&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"...there was a lot. But we just talked to Aimi and Kiseki, the tsukumogami, this morning. And it seems like, even though Aimi was trying to fulfill some of her own desires, at the bottom of it she really did want everyone else to be able to live their dreams too."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"...不少事情，但是我们今天刚和爱美和剪世树，那付丧神谈过了。看起来即使爱美一开始只是想要实现自己的梦想，但最后她确实是希望所有人梦想成真的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-63" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,63&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"We just had to stop them because they were going about it in the wrong way. Messing up Gensokyo's power balance, causing unexpected side effects in people's personalities, removing our free will...all that stuff."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我们因为这举动已经走向了错误的方向才不得不阻止她们的。她们不能搅乱幻想乡的力量平衡，随意改变人们的性格而禁锢他们的自由意志...之类的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-64" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,64&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I see."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我明白了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-65" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,65&#93;"><td id="铃仙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铃仙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Tetsuko was affected too, you know. She was annoyed by us at first, but somehow found that talking to all the incident-resolvers was interesting. The dream logic was making her think more about others."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"铁子也被影响了，你知道吗，她一开始觉得我们很烦，但是她很快发现找我们城管聊天是很有趣的。梦逻辑让她更为别人考虑了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-66" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,66&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Her personality was changed too, huh? So is Tetsuko a..."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"她的性格也被改变了？所以铁子是..."</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-67" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,67&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I'm a human. I lived in the Human Village as an adolescent, but for some reason I've always felt more comfortable around youkai than humans."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我是人类，之前少年的时候在村子里住，但是因为某些原因我总是觉得在妖怪身边更舒服。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-68" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,68&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"So when I needed to make myself useful in the village, I couldn't fit in because my way of thinking was more youkai-like. I tried desperately to understand other humans, and after a while I guess that manifested as an ability to read emotions."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"所以当时我想让自己在村庄里也做点贡献的时候，我因为思想更加像妖怪而无法融入，我绝望地尝试去理解其他人类，过了一段时间我发现自己拥有了阅读情绪的能力。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-69" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,69&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I thought that could be a skill for me to use, but no one really had a way for me to use it. Everyone just thought it was weird and creepy that I could tell what they were feeling."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我当时觉得这是个有用的技能，但是没人能找到我这个技能能用在哪里。大家只是觉得我能看透他们的感受而感到奇怪且不寒而栗。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-70" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,70&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I wasn't human enough to live with humans, and not youkai enough to become a youkai. There was nowhere for me to be, so I went to nowhere. This place. There's trees, leaves, flowers, and dirt here. I don't need anything else."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我太像妖怪了以至于我无法融入人类中，但也太过人类了而无法融入妖怪中，那在世界上哪里有我的容身之处呢？所以我来到了这里。这个地方，在这里没有其他人，只有树木，叶子，花朵和泥土，我在这里就足够了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-71" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,71&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Sanae dragged her shoe against the dirt awkwardly.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">早苗局促不安地把她的鞋子划过泥土。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-72" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,72&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"You're not sure what to say."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你不知道该说什么了对吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-73" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,73&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Correct."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"没错。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-74" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,74&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Reisen said she was sad to hear it too, but I told her she didn't need to be. There's nothing inadequate about my life here."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"铃仙说她听到这事也很伤心，但我告诉她没有什么可伤心的，我的生活在这里没有什么不好的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-75" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,75&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I guess I can understand that. I might give up on society too if I was in your place. But if Reisen's theory is correct, that means you must still have at least a fairly human-like mind, right?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我想我能理解这点，如果我是你的话我估计也会放弃社会。但如果铃仙的理论是正确的，那你还有不少人类的思想存在吧？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-76" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,76&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Um..."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"呃..."</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-77" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,77&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">She looked down at nothing in particular. Her thoughts seemed to be stuck. Finally she shook her head.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">她望向地面，视线并没有聚焦在哪一处，她的思想似乎卡住了。终于过了一会，她摇了摇头。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-78" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,78&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I don't know."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我不知道。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-79" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,79&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Well, you don't have to answer. I just wondered what you would think."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊你不需要回答，我只是好奇你会想什么。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-80" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,80&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I hope I'm not infringing on your comfort zone, Tetsuko, but I wonder if somewhere deep inside you there's still a desire to connect with others? My home is just up the mountain, at the Moriya Shrine. If you'd ever like to just, uh...see other people, maybe you could try worshipping at the shrine?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我希望我没有侵犯你的舒适区铁子，但我在想你是否还埋藏着希望与他人交流的思想呢？我的家就在山上的守矢神社，如果你想...见见其他人，那可以尝试去神社祭拜一下？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-81" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,81&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Tetsuko let out a sigh.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铁子叹了口气</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-82" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,82&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I'd still rather not be around people, but the whole dream logic experience did make me wonder about some things. I can...think about it. I guess."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我依旧不愿意呆在人们身边，但这梦逻辑给我的经历确实让我思考了一些事情，我觉得我会...考虑的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-83" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,83&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"All right. That sounds good to me. I come and go from the mountain pretty often, so just let me know if you want anything."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"好，听起来不错，我上山下山蛮频繁的，如果需要什么尽管和我说。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-84" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,84&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I will."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我会的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-85" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,85&#93;"><td id="铃仙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铃仙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I think I'll head home now, but I'm glad we could all leave off on a good note."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我想我该回家了，但我很高兴我们最后能欢笑着结束对话。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-86" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,86&#93;"><td id="东风谷早苗" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东风谷早苗</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Me too. I'll be seeing you, Reisen. And you too, Tetsuko."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我也该回家了，拜拜啦铃仙，还有铁子。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._04-87" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,87&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Tetsuko nodded. For an instant, Sanae thought she could see just the faintest hint of a smile on Tetsuko's face.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铁子点了点头，在那一瞬间，早苗发誓她看见铁子的嘴角露出了最浅的笑容。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Ending_No._04-88" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,88&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Intrinsic and Instrumental Value Team's Ending: "Friendships Forged by the Incident"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">工具与内在结局: "异变铸真情"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Ending_No._04-89" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 04&quot;,89&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Congratulations on a 1-credit clear!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">恭喜 1-credit 通关！</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
